0pt 12pt 0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Research and development (R&amp;D) expenses</b> totaled $4.0 million for the three&#160;months ended June&#160;30, 2023, compared to $2.6 million for the same period in 2022. The $1.4 million increase in R&amp;D expense was primarily due to increases in costs associated with preclinical studies, quality and clinical manufacturing as Gain&#8217;s GBA1 Parkinson&#8217;s disease program advances toward clinical trials. The increase in R&amp;D expense was also due to higher personnel-related costs associated with an increase in employee headcount.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-indent:0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">General and administrative (G&amp;A) expenses</b> totaled $3.7 million for the three&#160;months ended June&#160;30, 2023, compared to $2.7 million for the same period in 2022. The increase in G&amp;A expenses of $1.0 million was primarily due to higher legal fees, accounting, information technology costs and increased investor relations expenses. The increase in G&amp;A expenses was also due to an increase in personnel-related costs.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-indent:0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Net loss</b> for the three&#160;months ended June&#160;30, 2023, was $7.7 million, or $0.62 per share basic and diluted, including non-cash stock-based compensation expense of $1.3 million, compared to a net loss of $5.1 million, or $0.43 per share basic and diluted, which included non-cash stock-based compensation expense of $0.4 million for the period ended June&#160;30, 2022.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-indent:0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities</b> were $16.2 million as of June&#160;30, 2023, which the Company believes is sufficient to support operations into the third quarter of 2024.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New style="vertical-align:bottom;white-space:nowrap;width:11.36%;border-bottom:3px double #000000;margin:0pt;padding:0pt;"><p style="font-family:'Times New style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;">4</p></div></div><hr style="background-color:#000000;clear:both;color:#000000;height:2pt;line-height:0;margin-bottom:30pt;margin-left:10.35%;margin-right:10.35%;margin-top:30pt;page-break-after:always;width:79.3%;border-width:0;"><div style="max-width:100%;padding-left:10.35%;padding-right:10.35%;position:relative;"><div style="margin-top:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div><div style="clear:both;max-width:100%;position:relative;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt 0pt;">About Gain Therapeutics,&#160;Inc.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-indent:0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt 0pt;">Gain Therapeutics,&#160;Inc. is a biotechnology company leading the discovery and development of next generation allosteric therapies. Gain&#8217;s lead drug candidate GT-02287, in development for the treatment of GBA1 Parkinson&#8217;s disease, has completed IND-enabling GLP toxicology studies. Clinical evaluation of GT-02287 is expected to begin this&#160;year.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-indent:0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt 0pt;">Leveraging AI-supported structural biology, proprietary algorithms and supercomputer-powered physics-based models, the company&#8217;s SEE-Tx<sup style="font-size:7.5pt;vertical-align:top;">&#174;</sup> discovery platform can identify novel allosteric binding sites on disease-implicated proteins, pinpointing pockets that cannot be found or drugged with current technologies. Gain&#8217;s unique approach enables the discovery of novel, allosteric small molecule modulators that can restore or disrupt protein function. Deploying its highly advanced platform, Gain is accelerating drug discovery and unlocking novel disease-modifying treatments for untreatable or difficult-to-treat disorders including neurodegenerative diseases, rare genetic disorders and oncology. For more information, please visit <u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">GainTherapeutics.com</u> and follow us on <u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">LinkedIn</u>.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt 0pt;">Cautionary Note&#160;Regarding Forward-Looking Statements</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-indent:0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt 0pt;">This press release contains &quot;forward-looking statements&quot; within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="authRefData" style="display: none;" id="defref_dei_WrittenCommunications">
<tr><td class="hide"><a style="color: white;" href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="Show.hideAR();">X</a></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="body" style="padding: 2px;">
<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="Show.toggleNext( this );">- Definition</a><div><p>Boolean flag that is true when the Form 8-K filing is intended to satisfy the filing obligation of the registrant as written communications pursuant to Rule 425 under the Securities Act.</p></div>
